Get user from database\n        result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.id == user_id))\n        user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n        \n        if user is None:\n            raise AuthenticationError("User not found")\n        \n        if not user.is_active:\n            raise AuthenticationError("User account is inactive")\n        \n        return user\n        \n    except JWTError:\n        raise AuthenticationError("Invalid authentication credentials")\n\n\nasync def get_current_active_user(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current active user"""\n    if not current_user.is_active:\n        raise AuthenticationError("Inactive user")\n    return current_user\n\n\nasync def get_current_verified_user(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_active_user)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current verified user"""\n    if not current_user.is_verified:\n        raise AuthorizationError("Email verification required")\n    return current_user\n\n\nasync def get_current_premium_user(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_active_user)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current premium user"""\n    if current_user.role not in [UserRole.PREMIUM, UserRole.LIFETIME, UserRole.ORGANIZATION, UserRole.ADMIN]:\n        raise AuthorizationError("Premium subscription required")\n    return current_user\n\n\nasync def get_current_admin_user(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_active_user)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current admin user"""\n    if not current_user.is_superuser:\n        raise AuthorizationError("Admin privileges required")\n    return current_user\n\n\nasync def verify_api_key(\n    x_api_key: Optional[str] = Header(None),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> User:\n    """Verify API key and return associated user"""\n    if not x_api_key:\n        raise AuthenticationError("API key required")\n    \n    from app.models.user import APIKey\n    \n    # Check if user already exists\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.email == user_data.email))\n    existing_user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if existing_user:\n        raise ValidationError("Email already registered")\n    \n    # Validate password strength\n    if len(user_data.password) < 8:\n        raise ValidationError("Password must be at least 8 characters long")\n    \n    # Create new user\n    user = User(\n        email=user_data.email,\n        full_name=user_data.full_name,\n        hashed_password=get_password_hash(user_data.password),\n        role=UserRole.FREE,\n        subscription_status=SubscriptionStatus.TRIAL,\n        is_active=True,\n        is_verified=False\n    )\n    \n    db.add(user)\n    await db.commit()\n    await db.refresh(user)\n    \n    # Generate tokens\n    access_token = create_access_token({"sub": user.id})\n    refresh_token = create_refresh_token({"sub": user.id})\n    \n    # Send verification email (background task)\n    # background_tasks.add_task(send_verification_email, user.email)\n    \n    return {\n        "access_token": access_token,\n        "refresh_token": refresh_token,\n        "token_type": "bearer",\n        "user": {\n            "id": user.id,\n            "email": user.email,\n            "full_name": user.full_name,\n            "role": user.role,\n            "is_verified": user.is_verified\n        }\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/login", response_model=TokenResponse)\nasync def login(\n    user_data: UserLogin,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Login user"""\n    \n    # Get user by email\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.email == user_data.email))\n    user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not user or not verify_password(user_data.password, user.hashed_password):\n        raise AuthenticationError("Incorrect email or password")\n    \n    if not user.is_active:\n        raise AuthenticationError("Account is inactive")\n    \n    # Update last login\n    user.last_login_at = datetime.utcnow()\n    await db.commit()\n    \n    # Generate tokens\n    access_token = create_access_token({"sub": user.id})\n    refresh_token = create_refresh_token({"sub": user.id})\n    \n    return {\n        "access_token": access_token,\n        "refresh_token": refresh_token,\n        "token_type": "bearer",\n        "user": {\n            "id": user.id,\n            "email": user.email,\n            "full_name": user.full_name,\n            "role": user.role,\n            "is_verified": user.is_verified,\n            "subscription_status": user.subscription_status\n        }\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/refresh", response_model=TokenResponse)\nasync def refresh_token(\n    token_data: RefreshTokenRequest,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Refresh access token"""\n    \n    try:\n        payload = decode_token(token_data.refresh_token)\n        \n        if payload.get("type") != "refresh":\n            raise AuthenticationError("Invalid token type")\n        \n        user_id = payload.get("sub")\n        \n        # Get user\n        result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.id == user_id))\n        user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n        \n        if not user or not user.is_active:\n            raise AuthenticationError("Invalid token")\n        \n        # Generate new tokens\n        access_token = create_access_token({"sub": user.id})\n        refresh_token = create_refresh_token({"sub": user.id})\n        \n        return {\n            "access_token": access_token,\n            "refresh_token": refresh_token,\n            "token_type": "bearer",\n            "user": {\n                "id": user.id,\n                "email": user.email,\n                "full_name": user.full_name,\n                "role": user.role\n            }\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        raise AuthenticationError(f"Token refresh failed: {str(e)}")\n\n\n@router.post("/verify-email")\nasync def verify_email(\n    verification_data: VerifyEmailRequest,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Verify user email"""\n    \n    # In production, verify the code against stored verification codes\n    # For now, we\'ll just mark the user as verified\n    \n    return {\n        "message": "Email verified successfully",\n        "verified": True\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/forgot-password")\nasync def forgot_password(\n    request_data: ForgotPasswordRequest,\n    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Request password reset"""\n    \n    # Get user by email\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.email == request_data.email))\n    user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    # Always return success to prevent email enumeration\n    if user:\n        # Generate reset token\n        reset_token = create_access_token(\n            {"sub": user.id, "type": "password_reset"},\n            expires_delta=timedelta(hours=1)\n        )\n        \n        # Send reset email (background task)\n        # background_tasks.add_task(send_password_reset_email, user.email, reset_token)\n    \n    return {\n        "message": "If the email exists, a password reset link has been sent"\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/reset-password")\nasync def reset_password(\n    reset_data: ResetPasswordRequest,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Reset password with token"""\n    \n    try:\n        payload = decode_token(reset_data.token)\n        \n        if payload.get("type") != "password_reset":\n            raise AuthenticationError("Invalid token type")\n        \n        user_id = payload.get("sub")\n        \n        # Get user\n        result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.id == user_id))\n        user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n        \n        if not user:\n            raise AuthenticationError("Invalid token")\n        \n        # Validate new password\n        if len(reset_data.new_password) < 8:\n            raise ValidationError("Password must be at least 8 characters long")\n        \n        # Update password\n        user.hashed_password = get_password_hash(reset_data.new_password)\n        await db.commit()\n        \n        return {\n            "message": "Password reset successfully"\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        raise AuthenticationError(f"Password reset failed: {str(e)}")\n\n\n@router.post("/logout")\nasync def logout():\n    """Logout user (client-side token removal)"""\n    return {\n        "message": "Logged out successfully"\n    }\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="prooflink/backend/app/api/v1/mcp.py">\n"""\nMCP (Model Context Protocol) server endpoints\n"""\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel\nfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List\n\nfrom app.core.database import get_db\nfrom app.api.deps import get_current_user, verify_api_key\nfrom app.models.user import User\nfrom app.core.exceptions import MCPError\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n\n# Schemas\nclass MCPRequest(BaseModel):\n    function: str\n    params: Dict[str, Any]\n\n\nclass MCPResponse(BaseModel):\n    success: bool\n    result: Optional[Any] = None\n    error: Optional[str] = None\n\n\nclass MCPToolInfo(BaseModel):\n    name: str\n    description: str\n    parameters: Dict[str, Any]\n\n\n# MCP Functions\nasync def mcp_create_proof(params: Dict[str, Any], user: User, db: AsyncSession) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    """MCP function: create_proof"""\n    \n    from app.models.proof import Proof, ProofType, ProofStatus, VerificationMethod\n    from app.core.security import hash_file, generate_proof_link\n    from datetime import datetime\n    \n    # Extract parameters\n    file_hash = params.get("file_hash")\n    user_id = params.get("user_id", user.id)\n    timestamp = params.get("timestamp", datetime.utcnow().isoformat())\n    signature = params.get("signature")\n    \n    if not file_hash:\n        raise MCPError("file_hash is required")\n    \n    # Generate proof link\n    proof_link = generate_proof_link()\n    \n    # Create proof\n    proof = Proof(\n        user_id=user_id,\n        proof_link=proof_link,\n        proof_type=ProofType.FILE,\n        status=ProofStatus.VERIFIED,\n        file_hash=file_hash,\n        hash_algorithm="SHA256",\n        signature=signature,\n        timestamp=datetime.fromisoformat(timestamp) if isinstance(timestamp, str) else timestamp,\n        verification_method=VerificationMethod.HASH\n    )\n    \n    db.add(proof)\n    await db.commit()\n    await db.refresh(proof)\n    \n    return {\n        "proof_id": proof.id,\n        "proof_link": proof.proof_link,\n        "verification_url": f"https://prooflink.ai/verify/{proof.proof_link}"\n    }\n\n\nasync def mcp_verify_proof(params: Dict[str, Any], user: User, db: AsyncSession) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    """MCP function: verify_proof"""\n    \n    from app.models.proof import Proof\n    from sqlalchemy import select\n    \n    proof_link = params.get("proof_link")\n    \n    if not proof_link:\n        raise MCPError("proof_link is required")\n    \n    result = await db.execute(\n        select(Proof).where(Proof.proof_link == proof_link)\n    )\n    proof = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not proof:\n        return {\n            "verified": False,\n            "error": "Proof not found"\n        }\n    \n    return {\n        "verified": True,\n        "proof_id": proof.id,\n        "file_hash": proof.file_hash,\n        "timestamp": proof.timestamp.isoformat(),\n        "status": proof.status.value\n    }\n\n\nasync def mcp_get_user_proofs(params: Dict[str, Any], user: User, db: AsyncSession) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    """MCP function: get_user_proofs"""\n    \n    from app.models.proof import Proof\n    from sqlalchemy import select\n    \n    limit = params.get("limit", 10)\n    \n    result = await db.execute(\n        select(Proof)\n        .where(Proof.user_id == user.id)\n        .order_by(Proof.created_at.desc())\n        .limit(limit)\n    )\n    proofs = result.scalars().all()\n    \n    return {\n        "proofs": [\n            {\n                "id": proof.id,\n                "proof_link": proof.proof_link,\n                "file_name": proof.file_name,\n                "file_hash": proof.file_hash,\n                "timestamp": proof.timestamp.isoformat()\n            }\n            for proof in proofs\n        ]\n    }\n\n\n# MCP Function Registry\nMCP_FUNCTIONS = {\n    "create_proof": mcp_create_proof,\n    "verify_proof": mcp_verify_proof,\n    "get_user_proofs": mcp_get_user_proofs,\n}\n\n\n# Endpoints\n@router.get("/tools")\nasync def get_mcp_tools():\n    """Get available MCP tools"""\n    \n    return {\n        "tools": [\n            {\n                "name": "create_proof",\n                "description": "Create a new proof for a file or content",\n                "parameters": {\n                    "file_hash": {"type": "string", "required": True, "description": "SHA-256 hash of the file"},\n                    "user_id": {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "User ID (defaults to current user)"},\n                    "timestamp": {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "ISO-8601 timestamp"},\n                    "signature": {"type": "string", "required": False, "description": "Optional PGP signature"}\n                }\n            },\n            {\n                "name": "verify_proof",\n                "description": "Verify a proof by its link",\n                "parameters": {\n                    "proof_link": {"type": "string", "required": True, "description": "Proof link to verify"}\n                }\n            },\n            {\n                "name": "get_user_proofs",\n                "description": "Get user\'s proofs",\n                "parameters": {\n                    "limit": {"type": "integer", "required": False, "description": "Number of proofs to return (default: 10)"}\n                }\n            }\n        ]\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/execute", response_model=MCPResponse)\nasync def execute_mcp_function(\n    request: MCPRequest,\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Execute an MCP function"""\n    \n    function_name = request.function\n    params = request.params\n    \n    # Get function\n    function = MCP_FUNCTIONS.get(function_name)\n    \n    if not function:\n        raise MCPError(f"Unknown function: {function_name}")\n    \n    try:\n
